[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 092377579d0e2656[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run against the CSV parsing functionality in the codebase triggered a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmedium-severity Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m alert. The injected input caused[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Apache Tika `TextAndCSVParser` to attempt an outbound HTTPS connection to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`, which was caught by the `ServerSideRequestForgery` sanitizer, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that untrusted data can drive network requests.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing, the `TextAndCSVParser` component parsed a cell that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontained a URL-like input. This led to an outbound socket connection attempt over [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTTPS [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The built-in SSRF sanitizer flagged this as a security [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m — untrusted input is used to reach arbitrary [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork destinations, potentially exposing internal services or leaking sensitive [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer detects network calls at `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`checkSsrfSocket`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows the connection originating in [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser.processURL` → `processCell` → `parse`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Standard JDK networking [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Socket.connect`, `HttpsClient`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked without [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput sanitization or destination restrictions.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness `TextAndCSVParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` and `parseOne` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdrive the parser with untrusted data, revealing the SSRF potential.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Relevant code areas to investigate for a holistic view:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Apache Tika CSV parser methods:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParser.processURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParser.processCell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. SSRF defense logic in:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `ServerSideRequestForgery.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines around [0m[1;36m71[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m127[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness entry point:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParserFuzzer.parseOne[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – `[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis evaluation highlights that the CSV parser accepts and processes URL constructs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom input, resulting in external network calls that are currently only guarded by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe sanitizer during fuzzing. A thorough code review of URL handling paths and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork invocation points in the parser is recommended to fully assess SSRF [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexposure.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
